                                                Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

One Queen Size or Double Size Bed, located on the main floor.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!

                                                Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

One Double Size or Queen Size Bed, located on the main floor.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!

                                                Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

Double Size Bed, located in the lower basement level.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!

                                                Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

One Double Size bed, located on the main level.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!

                                              <!-- react-text: 2 -->                                              <!-- /react-text -->                                              <div data-reactid="3">
                                                Welcome…

We have a lovely brick home centrally located in the chic, hip and trendy Royal Oak | Berkley, with convenient access to I-696, I-75, Southfield, Lodge and all expressways, you can easily get to Detroit and surrounding areas.  We try our best to make our home a comfortable, convenient and safe place for you to stay and we're proud at our 200+ guests and their positive reviews.  We welcome you to stay.

Our home is pet-free and smoke-free.

The Neighborhood…

Royal Oak | Berkley is an up-scale suburb outside of Detroit.  It is extremely safe and in fact one of the safest neighborhoods you can find.  Neighbors are typically professionals and starting families.  Within a mile is Woodward Avenue, famous for the Woodward Dream Cruise, which boasts a variety of restaurants, bars, grocery stores and everything you could imagine.

Detroit Airport
…is about 45-90 minutes away depending upon traffic, as the Airport is located in the middle of nowhere.

Downtown Detroit, Windsor|Ontario Canada and the Detroit Casinos
…are a quick 15-20 minutes down highway I-75.

Beaumont Hospital
…is 5-10 minutes away, and even some neighbors walk to work there.

Other Hospitals | Rochester | Pontiac | Auburn Hills
…are 30-40 minutes away, if that's too long, consider our other listing “LakeHouse" which is closer to these

The Room…

One single or double size bed, located on either lower level or main floor.

Access…

Electronic access, come and go as you please.

The Home…

Fully stocked Living Room and Kitchen with TV, WiFi internet, dishes, pots, pans and more.  Towels, washer, dryer and even the laundry soap provided!

Parking…

One parking space is included.

Getting around…

Cars are very convenient.  Taxis and buses are not as convenient but we do have them.  Download the Smart Bus schedule and maps if you plan to use public transportation.

Book early to avoid disappointment.  Our rooms always fill up!

We look forward to hosting you and welcome to Michigan!

                                              <!-- react-text: 2 -->                                              <!-- /react-text -->                                              <div data-reactid="3">
                                                Welcome to Royal Oak / Berkley, Michigan.

Royal Oak / Berkley is a chic, trendy and lively suburb outside of Detroit.  It offers the benefits of being one of the safest neighborhoods in Michigan, with convenient access to everything.

Just a stones throw away is Woodward Avenue, the famous car street with 5 lanes each direction.  Here, you can find grocery, restaurants, bars, shopping and more.  Downtown Berkley, Royal Oak, Ferndale and Birmingham are all within 10-15 minutes drive.  It's really food galore!  Not to mention, convenient access to freeways 696 and 75, lodge, and southfield freeways.  Easy access to Detroit and pretty much anywhere.

The neighborhood is a tree-lined suburb comprising mostly of young professionals in their late 20's and 30's, along with beginning families.  The homes are typically bungalow style.

Our home has 5 bedrooms with 1 shared bathroom.  This listing is to rent the entire home, please note that you can check the calendar and pricing within the website, and those who are interested can make a booking request and we can entertain your requests.

There is one large room which is the entire upstairs with a king size bed.  Two bedrooms on the main floor with queen size beds.  Two bedrooms in the partially finished basement, one with a queen bed and the other with a futon. The basement bedrooms are partially finished.  The unfinished area of the basement has a washer and dryer.  Please note that basements sometimes are more humid, damp and/or wet. 

The kitchen is well maintained with full fridge, large newer sink and commercial style faucet, the bathroom is newer with the original tub and new rain shower with water jets.

The living room has a large TV with cable and wifi internet provided.  Pay per view channels are available at an additional fee.  There is a nice large sofa where another guest could stay.

The home features all appliances, stove, oven fridge/freezer, washer/dryer, central AC and heating, parking, 2 car garage.  Please note that parking on streets is not allowed by city ordinance, and only one car may pass thru the driveway at a time, hence parking can get a bit tricky if you have 5 or more cars.  There is a method to park in which it allows for everyone to gain access and we will explain that at check-in.

Car is recommended in Michigan as public transportation is not as reliable nor consistent.  Taxi is available but you must call ahead and request one.  Bus transportation is present but not recommended.

Airport pickup service is available for $100US.  The distance from the airport is about 45 minutes to 1 hour depending upon traffic and time of day.

Other premium services are available upon request.

Pets are allowed with a pet fee.  Smoking is not allowed in the house.  There is a front porch that you may sit on, enjoy some BBQ and enjoy the quiet and peaceful neighborhood and all it has to offer.

                                                    2015-05-26T00:00:00Z
                                                  </span>
                                                </li>
                                                <li data-reactid="34">
                                                  <p data-reactid="35">
                                                    The house was as described by Michael and Jessica, and by the majority of the reviewers.  We needed a location within walking distance of extended family in the Oak Park area, where our whole family (2 fifty-somethings, plus 4 young adults living in various locations across the U.S.) could stay together.  The Berkley Flower house fit this need perfectly.  It was nice having a place we could all  hang out together, rather than staying in a hotel (none are available in the immediate area anyway).  The house is also walking distance to Trader Joe's and Westborn, a wonderful local fresh produce and grocery market.    The house  is  inviting and welcoming, well decorated and equipped.  The living room, kitchen, and first and second floor, bedrooms are all very nice and comfortable.  The basement bedrooms seemed less so.  One is better (our non-fussy, 22 year old son thought it was totally fine and he stayed there).  The second basement bedroom even he admitted seemed somewhat dingy.  However, the whole house was very clean, including the basement.    Another minor downside is the bathroom.  It's up to date and modern, but is somewhat small. Plus with six people staying in the house, it would have been nice to have more than one.   With people on different schedules, this wouldn't matter.    Overall, would recommend this place and would stay there again, especially with the great location and lack of other lodging options in the area.

                                                Welcome to Michigan!  The land of the great lakes.

This listing brings you to the cities of Berkley and Royal Oak, just a 15-20 minute drive outside of Detroit.  Berkley and Royal Oak are unique in that they attract the young to middle aged blue and white collar working couples and families.

Berkley and Royal Oak are rated amongst the safest cities in the states, and provide you quick access to everything, downtown areas, restaurants, shopping, bars, grocery stores and more.

The home is a beautiful brick home with 1 large bedroom located upstairs with a king size bed.  On the main floor are 2 bedrooms with queen size beds, a living room with wall mounted plasma TV, gas fireplace, large sofa, kitchen, bathroom and dining room.

In the lower level there is the washer/dryer and two bedrooms with double size beds.  The lower level is not completely finished and tends to be a bit colder than the upper floors.

There are a total of 5 beds, and each bed in theory could hold 2 people, so this home could accommodate a maximum of 10 people.

We look forward to hosting you soon.
